<a id="18566" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="18568" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="18572" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4076" class="Function Operator">begin</a>
    <a id="18582" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#18488" class="Function">sucs</a> <a id="18587" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="18589" class="Number">0</a> <a id="18591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18593" class="Number">1</a> <a id="18595" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18597" class="Number">2</a> <a id="18599" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
  <a id="18603" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4134" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="18611" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#17306" class="Function">map</a> <a id="18615" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#128" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="18619" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="18621" class="Number">0</a> <a id="18623" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18625" class="Number">1</a> <a id="18627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18629" class="Number">2</a> <a id="18631" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
  <a id="18635" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4134" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="18643" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="18645" class="Number">1</a> <a id="18647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18649" class="Number">2</a> <a id="18651" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18653" class="Number">3</a> <a id="18655" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
  <a id="18659" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

{::comment}
Any type that is parameterised on another type, such as lists, has a
corresponding map, which accepts a function and returns a function
from the type parameterised on the domain of the function to the type
parameterised on the range of the function. Further, a type that is
parameterised on _n_ types will have a map that is parameterised on
_n_ functions.
{:/}

任何对于另外一个类型参数化的类型，例如列表，都有对应的映射，其接受一个函数，并返回另一个从由给定函数定义域参数化的类型，到由给定函数值域参数化的函数。除此之外，一个对于 _n_ 个类型参数化的类型会有一个对于 _n_ 个函数参数化的映射。

{::comment}
#### Exercise `map-compose`
{:/}

证明函数组合的映射是两个映射的组合：

{::comment}
## Fold {#Fold}
{:/}

## 折叠 {#Fold}

{::comment}
Fold takes an operator and a value, and uses the operator to combine
each of the elements of the list, taking the given value as the result
for the empty list:
{:/}

折叠取一个运算符和一个值，并使用运算符将列表中的元素合并至一个值，如果给定的列表为空，则使用给定的值：
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="foldr"></a><a id="20673" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20673" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="20679" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20681" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="20683" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20684" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20684" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20686" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20686" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="20688" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20690" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="20693" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20695" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20697" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20698" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20684" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20700" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20702" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20686" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="20704" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20706" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20686" class="Bound">B</a><a id="20707" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20709" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20686" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="20713" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20715" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1325" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="20720" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20684" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20722" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20724" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20686" class="Bound">B</a>
<a id="20726" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20673" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="20732" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20732" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="20736" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20736" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="20738" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1354" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>        <a id="20748" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="20751" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20736" class="Bound">e</a>

{::comment}
Fold of the empty list is the given value.
Fold of a non-empty list uses the operator to combine
the head of the list and the fold of the tail of the list.
{:/}

空列表的折叠是给定的值。非空列表的折叠使用给定的运算符，将头元素和尾列表的折叠合并起来。

{::comment}
Here is an example showing how to use fold to find the sum of a list:
{:/}

下面的例子展示了如何使用折叠来对一个列表求和：

{::comment}
Fold requires time linear in the length of the list.
{:/}

折叠需要关于列表长度线性的时间。

{::comment}
It is often convenient to exploit currying by applying
fold to an operator and a value to yield a new function,
and at a later point applying the resulting function:
{:/}

我们常常可以利用柯里化，将折叠作用于一个运算符和一个值，获得另一个函数，然后在之后的时候应用获得的函数：
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="sum"></a><a id="21813" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#21813" class="Function">sum</a> <a id="21817" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21819" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1325" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="21824" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#97" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="21826" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21828" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#97" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

  <a id="21886" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4076" class="Function Operator">begin</a>

  <a id="21960" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4134" class="Function Operator">≡⟨⟩</a>
    <a id="21968" class="Number">10</a>
  <a id="21973" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

{::comment}
Just as the list type has two constructors, `[]` and `_∷_`,
so the fold function takes two arguments, `e` and `_⊗_`
(in addition to the list argument).
In general, a data type with _n_ constructors will have
a corresponding fold function that takes _n_ arguments.
{:/}

正如列表由两个构造器 `[]` 和 `_∷_`，折叠函数取两个参数 `e` 和 `_⊗_`
（除去列表参数）。推广来说，一个有 _n_ 个构造器的数据类型，会有对应的取 _n_ 个参数的折叠函数。

{::comment}
#### Exercise `product` (recommended)
{:/}

#### 练习 `product` （推荐）

{::comment}
Use fold to define a function to find the product of a list of numbers.
For example:
{:/}

使用折叠来定义一个计算列表数字之积的函数。例如：

    product [ 1 , 2 , 3 , 4 ] ≡ 24

{::comment}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="22640" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
{:/}

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="22693" class="Comment">-- 请将代码写在此处。</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

{::comment}
#### Exercise `foldr-++` (recommended)
{:/}

#### 练习 `foldr-++` （推荐）

{::comment}
Show that fold and append are related as follows:
{:/}

{::comment}
## Monoids
{:/}

## 幺半群

{::comment}
Typically when we use a fold the operator is associative and the
value is a left and right identity for the operator, meaning that the
operator and the value form a _monoid_.
{:/}

一般来说，我们会对于折叠函数使用一个满足结合律的运算符，和这个运算符的左右幺元。这意味着这个运算符和这个值形成了一个**幺半群**（Monoid）。

{::comment}
We can define a monoid as a suitable record type:
{:/}

我们可以用一个合适的记录类型来定义幺半群：
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="25092" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="IsMonoid"></a><a id="25099" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25099" class="Record">IsMonoid</a> <a id="25108" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25109" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25109" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25111" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25113" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="25116" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="25118" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25119" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25119" class="Bound Operator">_⊗_</a> <a id="25123" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25125" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25109" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25127" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25129" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25109" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25131" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25133" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25109" class="Bound">A</a><a id="25134" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25136" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25137" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25137" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="25139" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25141" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25109" class="Bound">A</a><a id="25142" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25144" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25146" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="25150" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="25158" class="Keyword">field</a>
    <a id="IsMonoid.assoc"></a><a id="25168" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25168" class="Field">assoc</a> <a id="25174" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25176" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="25178" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25179" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25179" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="25181" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25181" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="25183" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25183" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="25185" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25187" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25109" class="Bound">A</a><a id="25188" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25190" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25192" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25193" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25179" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="25195" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25119" class="Bound Operator">⊗</a> <a id="25197" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25181" class="Bound">y</a><a id="25198" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25200" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25119" class="Bound Operator">⊗</a> <a id="25202" href="{% <a id="25295" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="25300" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#25099" class="Module">IsMonoid</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

{::comment}
As examples, sum and zero, multiplication and one, and append and the empty
list, are all examples of monoids:
{:/}

举例来说，加法和零，乘法和一，附加和空列表，都是幺半群：

{::comment}
If `_⊗_` and `e` form a monoid, then we can re-express fold on the
same operator and an arbitrary value:
{:/}


如果 `_⊗_` 和 `e` 构成一个幺半群，那么我们可以用相同的运算符和一个任意的值来表示折叠：

{::comment}
#### Exercise `foldl`
{:/}

#### 练习 `foldl`

{::comment}
Define a function `foldl` which is analogous to `foldr`, but where
operations associate to the left rather than the right.  For example:
{:/}

定义一个函数 `foldl`，与 `foldr` 相似，但是运算符向左结合，而不是向右。例如：

    foldr _⊗_ e [ x , y , z ]  =  x ⊗ (y ⊗ (z ⊗ e))
    foldl _⊗_ e [ x , y , z ]  =  ((e ⊗ x) ⊗ y) ⊗ z

{::comment}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="27642" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
{:/}

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="27695" class="Comment">-- 请将代码写在此处。</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


{::comment}
#### Exercise `foldr-monoid-foldl`
{:/}

#### 练习 `foldr-monoid-foldl`

{::comment}
Show that if `_⊗_` and `e` form a monoid, then `foldr _⊗_ e` and
`foldl _⊗_ e` always compute the same result.
{:/}

证明如果 `_⊗_` 和 `e` 构成幺半群，那么 `foldr _⊗_ e` 和 `foldl _⊗_ e` 的结果永远是相同的。

{::comment}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="28027" class="Comment">-- Your code goes here</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
{:/}

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="28080" class="Comment">-- 请将代码写在此处。</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


{::comment}
## All {#All}
{:/}

## 所有 {#All}

{::comment}
We can also define predicates over lists. Two of the most important
are `All` and `Any`.
{:/}

我们也可以定义关于列表的谓词。最重要的两个谓词是 `All` 和 `Any`。

{::comment}
Predicate `All P` holds if predicate `P` is satisfied by every element of a list:
{:/}

谓词 `All P` 当列表里的所有元素满足 `P` 时成立：
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="28445" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="All"></a><a id="28450" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28450" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="28454" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28455" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28455" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28457" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28459" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="28462" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28464" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28465" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28465" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="28467" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28469" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28455" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28471" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28473" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="28476" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28478" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28480" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1325" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="28485" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28455" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28487" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28489" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="28493" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="All.[]"></a><a id="28501" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28501" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>  <a id="28505" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28507" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28450" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="28511" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28465" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="28513" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1354" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>
  <a id="All._∷_"></a><a id="28518" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28518" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_∷_</a> <a id="28522" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28524" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="28526" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28527" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28527" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="28529" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28531" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28455" class="Bound">A</a><a id="28532" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28534" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28535" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28535" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="28538" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28540" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1325" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="28545" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28455" class="Bound">A</a><a id="28546" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28548" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28550" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28465" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="28552" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28527" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="28554" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28556" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28450" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="28560" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28465" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="28562" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28535" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="28565" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28567" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28450" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="28571" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28465" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="28573" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28574" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28527" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="28576" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1369" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="28578" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28535" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="28580" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
{::comment}
The type has two constructors, reusing the names of the same constructors for lists.
The first asserts that `P` holds for every element of the empty list.
The second asserts that if `P` holds of the head of a list and for every
element of the tail of a list, then `P` holds for every element of the list.
Agda uses types to disambiguate whether the constructor is building
a list or evidence that `All P` holds.
{:/}

这个类型有两个构造器，使用了与列表构造器相同的名称。第一个断言了 `P` 对于空列表的任何元素成立。第二个断言了如果 `P` 对于列表的头元素和尾列表的所有元素成立，那么 `P` 对于这个列表的任何元素成立。
Agda 使用类型来区分构造器是用于构造一个列表，还是构造 `All P` 成立的证明。

{::comment}
For example, `All (_≤ 2)` holds of a list where every element is less
than or equal to two.  Recall that `z≤n` proves `zero ≤ n` for any
`n`, and that if `m≤n` proves `m ≤ n` then `s≤s m≤n` proves `suc m ≤
suc n`, for any `m` and `n`:
{:/}

比如说，`All (_≤ 2)` 对于一个每一个元素都小于等于二的列表成立。回忆 `z≤n` 证明了对于任意 `n`， `zero ≤ n` 成立；对于任意 `m` 和 `n`，如果 `m≤n` 证明了 `m ≤ n`，那么 `s≤s m≤n` 证明了 `suc m ≤
suc n`:
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="29587" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#29587" class="Function">_</a> <a id="29589" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="29591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28450" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="29595" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29596" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Nat.Base.html#845" class="Datatype Operator">_≤</a> <a id="29599" class="Number">2</a><a id="29600" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29602" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="29604" class="Number">0</a> <a id="29606" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="29608" class="Number">1</a> <a id="29610" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="29612" class="Number">2</a> <a id="29614" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#3975" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
<a id="29616" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="29618" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="29620" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Nat.Base.html#868" class="InductiveConstructor">z≤n</a> <a id="29624" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28518" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="29626" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Nat.Base.html#910" class="InductiveConstructor">s≤s</a> <a id="29630" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Nat.Base.html#868" class="InductiveConstructor">z≤n</a> <a id="29634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28518" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="29636" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Nat.Base.html#910" class="InductiveConstructor">s≤s</a> <a id="29640" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="29641" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Nat.Base.html#910" class="InductiveConstructor">s≤s</a> <a id="29645" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Nat.Base.html#868" class="InductiveConstructor">z≤n</a><a id="29648" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="29650" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28518" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="29652" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28501" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
{::comment}
Here `_∷_` and `[]` are the constructors of `All P` rather than of `List A`.
The three items are proofs of `0 ≤ 2`, `1 ≤ 2`, and `2 ≤ 2`, respectively.
{:/}

这里 `_∷_` 和 `[]` 是 `All P` 的构造器，而不是 `List A` 的。这三项分别是 `0 ≤ 2`、 `1 ≤ 2` 和 `2 ≤ 2` 的证明。

{::comment}
(One might wonder whether a pattern such as `[_,_,_]` can be used to
construct values of type `All` as well as type `List`, since both use
the same constructors. Indeed it can, so long as both types are in
scope when the pattern is declared.  That's not the case here, since
`List` is defined before `[_,_,_]`, but `All` is defined later.)
{:/}

（读者可能会思考诸如 `[_,_,_]` 的模式是否可以用于构造 `All` 类型的值，像构造 `List` 类型的一样，因为两者使用了相同的构造器。事实上这样做是可以的，只要两个类型在模式声明时在作用域内。然而现在不是这样的情况，因为 `List` 先于 `[_,_,_]` 定义，而 `All` 在之后定义。）

{::comment}
## Any
{:/}

## 任意

{::comment}
Predicate `Any P` holds if predicate `P` is satisfied by some element of a list:
{:/}

谓词 `Any P` 当列表里的一些元素满足 `P` 时成立：

class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="30788" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30751" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="30790" class="Symbol">)</a>{% {::comment}
The first constructor provides evidence that the head of the list
satisfies `P`, while the second provides evidence that some element of
the tail of the list satisfies `P`.  For example, we can define list
membership as follows:
{:/}

第一个构造器证明了列表的头元素满足 `P`，第二个构造器证明的列表的尾列表中的一些元素满足 `P`。举例来说，我们可以如下定义列表的成员关系：
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="31136" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="31142" class="Number">4</a> <a id="31144" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31153" class="Function Operator">_∈_</a> <a id="31148" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31223" class="Function Operator">_∉_</a>

<a id="_∈_"></a><a id="31153" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31153" class="Function Operator">_∈_</a> <a id="31157" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31159" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="31161" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31162" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31162" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="31164" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31166" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="31169" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31171" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31172" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31172" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="31174" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31176" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31162" class="Bound">A</a><a id="31177" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31179" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31180" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31180" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="31183" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31185" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1325" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="31190" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31162" class="Bound">A</a><a id="31191" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31193" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31195" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="31199" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31199" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="31201" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31153" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="31203" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31203" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="31206" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="31208" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30624" class="Datatype">Any</a> <a id="31212" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31213" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31199" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="31215" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#83" class="Datatype Operator">≡_</a><a id="31217" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31219" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31203" class="Bound">xs</a>

<a id="_∉_"></a><a id="31223" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31223" class="Function Operator">_∉_</a> <a id="31227" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31229" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="31231" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31232" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31232" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="31234" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31236" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="31239" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31241" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31242" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31242" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="31244" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31246" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31232" class="Bound">A</a><a id="31247" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31249" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31250" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31250" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="31253" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31255" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1325" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="31260" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31232" class="Bound">A</a><a id="31261" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="31263" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="31265" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="31269" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31269" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="31271" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31223" class="Function Operator">∉</a> <a id="31273" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31273" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="31276" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="31278" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="31280" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31281" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31269" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="31283" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31153" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="31285" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31273" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="31287" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
{::comment}
For example, zero is an element of the list `[ 0 , 1 , 0 , 2 ]`.  Indeed, we can demonstrate
this fact in two different ways, corresponding to the two different
occurrences of zero in the list, as the first element and as the third element:
{:/}

比如说，零是列表 `[ 0 , 1 , 0 , 2 ]` 中的一个元素。我们可以用两种方法来展示这个事实，对应零在列表中出现了两次：第一个元素和第三个元素：

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="31653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31653" class="Function">_</a> <a id="31655" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31657" class="Number">0</a> <a id="31659" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31153" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="31661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4014" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="31663" class="Number">0</a> <a id="31665" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4014" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="31667" class="Number">1</a> <a id="31669" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4014" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="31671" class="Number">0</a> <a id="31673" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4014" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="31675" class="Number">2</a> <a id="31677" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4014" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
<a id="31679" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="31681" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="31683" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30675" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a> <a id="31688" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

<a id="31694" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31694" class="Function">_</a> <a id="31696" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31698" class="Number">0</a> <a id="31700" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31153" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="31702" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4014" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="31704" class="Number">0</a> <a id="31706" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4014" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="31708" class="Number">1</a> <a id="31710" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4014" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="31712" class="Number">0</a> <a id="31714" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4014" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="31716" class="Number">2</a> <a id="31718" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4014" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
<a id="31720" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="31722" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="31724" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30732" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="31730" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31731" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30732" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="31737" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="31738" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30675" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a> <a id="31743" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="31747" class="Symbol">))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
{::comment}
Further, we can demonstrate that three is not in the list, because
any possible proof that it is in the list leads to contradiction:
{:/}

除此之外，我们可以展示三不在列表之中，因为任何它在列表中的证明会推导出矛盾：
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-in"></a><a id="31964" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31964" class="Function">not-in</a> <a id="31971" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31973" class="Number">3</a> <a id="31975" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31223" class="Function Operator">∉</a> <a id="31977" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4014" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">[</a> <a id="31979" class="Number">0</a> <a id="31981" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4014" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="31983" class="Number">1</a> <a id="31985" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4014" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="31987" class="Number">0</a> <a id="31989" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4014" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="31991" class="Number">2</a> <a id="31993" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4014" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">]</a>
<a id="31995" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31964" class="Function">not-in</a> <a id="32002" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32003" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30675" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a> <a id="32008" class="Symbol">())</a>
<a id="32012" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31964" class="Function">not-in</a> <a id="32019" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32020" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30732" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="32026" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32027" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30675" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a> <a id="32032" class="Symbol">()))</a>
<a id="32037" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31964" class="Function">not-in</a> <a id="32044" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32045" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30732" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="32051" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32052" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30732" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="32058" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32059" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30675" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a> <a id="32064" class="Symbol">())))</a>
<a id="32070" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31964" class="Function">not-in</a> <a id="32077" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32078" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30732" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="32084" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32085" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30732" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="32091" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32092" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30732" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="32098" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32099" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30675" class="InductiveConstructor">here</a> <a id="32104" class="Symbol">()))))</a>
<a id="32111" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#31964" class="Function">not-in</a> <a id="32118" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32119" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30732" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="32125" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32126" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30732" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="32132" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32133" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30732" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="32139" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32140" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30732" class="InductiveConstructor">there</a> <a id="32146" class="Symbol">()))))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
{::comment}
The five occurrences of `()` attest to the fact that there is no
possible evidence for `3 ≡ 0`, `3 ≡ 1`, `3 ≡ 0`, `3 ≡ 2`, and
`3 ∈ []`, respectively.
{:/}

`()` 出现了五次，分别表示没有 `3 ≡ 0`、 `3 ≡ 1`、 `3 ≡ 0`、 `3 ≡ 2` 和
`3 ∈ []` 的证明。

{::comment}
## All and append
{:/}

## 所有和附加

{::comment}
A predicate holds for every element of one list appended to another if and
only if it holds for every element of both lists:
{:/}

一个谓词对两个附加在一起的列表的每个元素都成立，当且仅当这个谓词对两个列表的每个元素都成立：
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="All-++-⇔"></a><a id="32652" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#32652" class="Function">All-++-⇔</a> <a id="32661" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32663" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="32665" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="32666" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#32666" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="32668" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32670" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="32673" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="32675" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="32676" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#32676" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="32678" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32680" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#32666" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="32682" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="32684" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="32687" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="32689" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32690" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#32690" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="32693" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#32693" class="Bound">ys</a> <a id="32696" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="32698" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1325" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="32703" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#32666" class="Bound">A</a><a id="32704" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32706" class="Symbol">→</a>
  <a id="32710" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28450" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="32714" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#32676" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="32716" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32717" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#32690" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="32720" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#4769" class="Function Operator">++</a> <a id="32723" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#32693" class="Bound">ys</a><a id="32725" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="32727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Isomorphism.md %}{% raw %}#15182" class="Record Operator">⇔</a> <a id="32729" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="32730" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28450" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="32734" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#32676" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="32736" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#32690" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="32739" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="32741" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28450" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="32745" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#32676" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="32747" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#32693" class="Bound">ys</a><a id="32749" class="Symbol">)</a>

{::comment}
#### Exercise `Any-++-⇔` (recommended)
{:/}

#### 练习 `Any-++-⇔` （推荐）

{::comment}
Prove a result similar to `All-++-⇔`, but with `Any` in place of `All`, and a suitable
replacement for `_×_`.  As a consequence, demonstrate an equivalence relating
`_∈_` and `_++_`.
{:/}
使用 `Any` 代替 `All` 与一个合适的 `_×_` 的替代，证明一个类似于 `All-++-⇔` 的结果。作为结论，展示关联 `_∈_` 和 `_++_` 的一个等价关系。

{:/}

#### Exercise `¬Any≃All¬` (stretch)
{:/}

#### 练习 `¬Any≃All¬` （拓展）

[universe polymorphism]({{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Equality.md%}#unipoly):

  <a id="34403" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34405" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34406" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34376" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="34408" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34410" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34389" class="Bound">C</a><a id="34411" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34413" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34415" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34416" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34363" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34418" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34420" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34376" class="Bound">B</a><a id="34421" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34423" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34425" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34363" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34427" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34429" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34389" class="Bound">C</a>
<a id="34431" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34432" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34432" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="34434" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34334" class="Function Operator">∘′</a> <a id="34437" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34437" class="Bound">f</a><a id="34438" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34440" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34440" class="Bound">x</a>  <a id="34443" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="34446" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34432" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="34448" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34449" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34437" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="34451" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34440" class="Bound">x</a><a id="34452" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

{::comment}
Show that `Any` and `All` satisfy a version of De Morgan's Law:
{:/}

证明 `Any` 和 `All` 满足某个形式的德摩根定律：
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="34592" class="Keyword">postulate</a>
  <a id="¬Any≃All¬"></a><a id="34604" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34604" class="Postulate">¬Any≃All¬</a> <a id="34614" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34616" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="34618" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="34619" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34619" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34621" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34623" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="34626" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="34628" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34629" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34629" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="34631" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34633" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34619" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34635" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34637" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="34640" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34642" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34643" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34643" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="34646" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34648" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1325" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="34653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34619" class="Bound">A</a><a id="34654" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="34660" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34662" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34663" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬_</a> <a id="34666" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34334" class="Function Operator">∘′</a> <a id="34669" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#30624" class="Datatype">Any</a> <a id="34673" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34629" class="Bound">P</a><a id="34674" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34676" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34643" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="34679" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Isomorphism.md %}{% raw %}#5561" class="Record Operator">≃</a> <a id="34681" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28450" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="34685" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34686" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬_</a> <a id="34689" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34334" class="Function Operator">∘′</a> <a id="34692" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34629" class="Bound">P</a><a id="34693" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34695" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34643" class="Bound">xs</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

{::comment}
Do we also have the following?
{:/}

下列命题是否成立？

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="34783" class="Keyword">postulate</a>
  <a id="¬All≃Any¬"></a><a id="34795" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34795" class="Postulate">¬All≃Any¬</a> <a id="34805" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34807" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="34809" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="34810" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34810" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34812" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34814" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="34817" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="34819" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34820" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34820" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="34822" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34824" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34810" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34826" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34828" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="34831" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34833" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34834" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34834" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="34837" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34839" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1325" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="34844" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#34810" class="Bound">A</a><a id="34845" class="Symbol">)</a>

{::comment}
If so, prove; if not, explain why.
{:/}

如果成立，请证明；如果不成立，请解释原因。


{::comment}
## Decidability of All
{:/}

## 所有的可判定性

{::comment}
If we consider a predicate as a function that yields a boolean,
it is easy to define an analogue of `All`, which returns true if
a given predicate returns true for every element of a list:
{:/}

如果我们将一个谓词看作一个返回布尔值的函数，那么我们可以简单的定义一个类似于 `All`
的函数，其当给定谓词对于列表每个元素返回真时返回真：

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="all"></a><a id="35323" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#35323" class="Function">all</a> <a id="35327" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35329" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="35331" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35332" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#35332" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35334" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35336" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="35339" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35341" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35343" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35344" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#35332" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35346" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35348" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Bool.html#67" class="Datatype">Bool</a><a id="35352" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35354" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35356" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1325" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="35361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#35332" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35363" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35365" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Bool.html#67" class="Datatype">Bool</a>
<a id="35370" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#35323" class="Function">all</a> <a id="35374" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#35374" class="Bound">p</a>  <a id="35377" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="35380" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#20673" class="Function">foldr</a> <a id="35386" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Data.Bool.Base.html#1012" class="Function Operator">_∧_</a> <a id="35390" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Agda.Builtin.Bool.html#92" class="InductiveConstructor">true</a> <a id="35395" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Function.html#769" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="35397" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#17306" class="Function">map</a> <a id="35401" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#35374" class="Bound">p</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
{::comment}
The function can be written in a particularly compact style by
using the higher-order functions `map` and `foldr`.
{:/}

我们可以使用高阶函数 `map` 和 `foldr` 来简洁地写出这个函数。

{::comment}
As one would hope, if we replace booleans by decidables there is again
an analogue of `All`.  First, return to the notion of a predicate `P` as
a function of type `A → Set`, taking a value `x` of type `A` into evidence
`P x` that a property holds for `x`.  Say that a predicate `P` is _decidable_
if we have a function that for a given `x` can decide `P x`:
{:/}

正如所希望的那样，如果我们将布尔值替换成可判定值，这与 `All` 是相似的。首先，回到将 `P`
当作一个类型为 `A → Set` 的函数的概念，将一个类型为 `A` 的值 `x` 转换成 `P x` 对 `x` 成立的证明。我们成 `P` 为**可判定的**（Decidable），如果我们有一个函数，其在给定 `x` 时能够判定 `P x`：

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Decidable"></a><a id="36155" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36155" class="Function">Decidable</a> <a id="36165" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="36167" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="36169" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="36170" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36170" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="36172" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="36174" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="36177" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="36179" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36181" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36182" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36170" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="36184" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36186" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="36189" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36191" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36193" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="36197" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36155" class="Function">Decidable</a> <a id="36207" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="36208" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36208" class="Bound">A</a><a id="36209" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="36211" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36211" class="Bound">P</a>  <a id="36214" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="36217" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="36219" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36220" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36220" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="36222" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="36224" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36208" class="Bound">A</a><a id="36225" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36227" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36229" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#534" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="36233" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36234" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36211" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="36236" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36220" class="Bound">x</a><a id="36237" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
{::comment}
Then if predicate `P` is decidable, it is also decidable whether every
element of a list satisfies the predicate:
{:/}

那么当谓词 `P` 可判定时，我们亦可判定列表中的每一个元素是否满足这个谓词：
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="All?"></a><a id="36435" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36435" class="Function">All?</a> <a id="36440" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="36442" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="36444" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="36445" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36445" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="36447" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="36449" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="36452" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="36454" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="36455" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36455" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="36457" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="36459" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36445" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="36461" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36463" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="36466" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="36468" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36470" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36155" class="Function">Decidable</a> <a id="36480" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36455" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="36482" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36484" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36155" class="Function">Decidable</a> <a id="36494" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36495" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28450" class="Datatype">All</a> <a id="36499" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36455" class="Bound">P</a><a id="36500" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="36502" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36435" class="Function">All?</a> <a id="36507" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36507" class="Bound">P?</a> <a id="36510" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1354" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>                                 <a id="36545" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="36548" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#570" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="36552" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28501" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a>
<a id="36555" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36435" class="Function">All?</a> <a id="36560" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36560" class="Bound">P?</a> <a id="36563" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36564" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36564" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="36566" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#1369" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="36568" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36568" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="36570" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36572" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="36577" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36560" class="Bound">P?</a> <a id="36580" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36564" class="Bound">x</a>   <a id="36584" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="36586" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36435" class="Function">All?</a> <a id="36591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36560" class="Bound">P?</a> <a id="36594" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36568" class="Bound">xs</a>

<a id="36658" class="Symbol">...</a>                 <a id="36678" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="36680" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#597" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="36683" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36683" class="Bound">¬Px</a> <a id="36687" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="36689" class="Symbol">_</a>           <a id="36701" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="36704" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#597" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="36707" class="Symbol">λ{</a> <a id="36710" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36711" class="Bound">Px</a> <a id="36714" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28518" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="36716" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36716" class="Bound">Pxs</a><a id="36719" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36721" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36723" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36683" class="Bound">¬Px</a> <a id="36727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36711" class="Bound">Px</a>   <a id="36732" class="Symbol">}</a>
<a id="36734" class="CatchallClause Symbol">...</a><a id="36737" class="CatchallClause">                 </a><a id="36754" class="CatchallClause Symbol">|</a><a id="36755" class="CatchallClause"> </a><a id="36756" class="CatchallClause Symbol">_</a><a id="36757" class="CatchallClause">      </a><a id="36763" class="CatchallClause Symbol">|</a><a id="36764" class="CatchallClause"> </a><a id="36765" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#597" class="CatchallClause InductiveConstructor">no</a><a id="36767" class="CatchallClause"> </a><a id="36768" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36768" class="CatchallClause Bound">¬Pxs</a>     <a id="36777" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="36780" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Nullary.html#597" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="36783" class="Symbol">λ{</a> <a id="36786" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36787" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36787" class="Bound">Px</a> <a id="36790" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#28518" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="36792" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36792" class="Bound">Pxs</a><a id="36795" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36797" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36799" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36768" class="Bound">¬Pxs</a> <a id="36804" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lists.md %}{% raw %}#36792" class="Bound">Pxs</a> <a id="36808" class="Symbol">}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
{::comment}
If the list is empty, then trivially `P` holds for every element of
the list.  Otherwise, the structure of the proof is similar to that
showing that the conjunction of two decidable propositions is itself
decidable, using `_∷_` rather than `⟨_,_⟩` to combine the evidence for
the head and tail of the list.
{:/}

如果列表为空，那么 `P` 显然对列表的每个元素成立。否则，证明的结构与两个可判定的命题是可判定的证明相似，不过我们使用 `_∷_` 而不是 `⟨_,_⟩`
来整合头元素和尾列表的证明。


{::comment}
#### Exercise `any?` (stretch)
{:/}

#### 练习 `any?` （延伸）

{::comment}
Just as `All` has analogues `all` and `All?` which determine whether a
predicate holds for every element of a list, so does `Any` have
analogues `any` and `Any?` which determine whether a predicate holds
for some element of a list.  Give their definitions.
{:/}

正如 `All` 有类似的 `all` 和 `All?` 形式，来判断列表的每个元素是否满足给定的谓词，那么 `Any` 也有类似的 `any` 和 `Any?` 形式，来判断列表的一些元素是否满足给定的谓词。给出它们的定义。

{:/}

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="37783" class="Comment">-- 请将代码写在此处。</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

#### Exercise `All-∀`
{:/}

#### 练习 `All-∀`

{::comment}
Show that `All P xs` is isomorphic to `∀ {x} → x ∈ xs → P x`.
{:/}

证明 `All P xs` 与 `∀ {x} → x ∈ xs → P x` 同构。

{::comment}

{:/}

{::comment}
#### Exercise `Any-∃`
{:/}

#### 练习 `Any-∃`

{::comment}
Show that `Any P xs` is isomorphic to `∃[ x ∈ xs ] P x`.
{:/}

证明 `Any P xs` 与 `∃[ x ∈ xs ] P x` 同构。

<a id="39445" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="39452" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Binary.html" class="Module">Relation.Binary</a> <a id="39468" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="39474" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="39475" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v0.17/Relation.Binary.Core.html#4499" class="Function">Decidable</a><a id="39484" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
{::comment}
The standard library version of `IsMonoid` differs from the
one given here, in that it is also parameterised on an equivalence relation.
{:/}

标准库中的 `IsMonoid` 与给出的定义不同，因为它可以针对特定的等价关系参数化。

{::comment}
Both `Relation.Unary` and `Relation.Binary` define a version of `Decidable`,
one for unary relations (as used in this chapter where `P` ranges over
unary predicates) and one for binary relations (as used earlier, where `_≤_`
ranges over a binary relation).
{:/}

`Relation.Unary` 和 `Relation.Binary` 都定义了 `Decidable` 的某个版本，一个用于单元关系（正如本章中的单元谓词 `P`），一个用于二元关系（正如之前使用的 `_≤_`）。

## Unicode

{::comment}
This chapter uses the following unicode:
{:/}

本章节使用下列 Unicode：

{::comment}
    ∷  U+2237  PROPORTION  (\::)
    ⊗  U+2297  CIRCLED TIMES  (\otimes, \ox)
    ∈  U+2208  ELEMENT OF  (\in)
    ∉  U+2209  NOT AN ELEMENT OF  (\inn, \notin)

{:/}

    ∷  U+2237  比例  (\::)
    ⊗  U+2297  带圈的乘号  (\otimes, \ox)
    ∈  U+2208  是……的元素  (\in)
    ∉  U+2209  不是……的元素  (\inn, \notin)
